<script type="text/javascript">
    $(document).ready(function() {
        $('.header-wrap-apk').addClass('display_block');
        const TIMESTAMP_MODEL = {
            initial: null,
            expiresOn: null
        };
        const TIMESTAMP = Date.now();
        if(JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('setupTime'))) {
            const EXPIRE_DATE = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('setupTime')).expiresOn;
            if (Date.now() > EXPIRE_DATE) {
                localStorage.clear();
            }
        }

        $('#close_download_apk_notification').click(function(){
            $('.download-apk-notification').addClass('none');
            $('body').addClass('body_change');
            $('.header-wrap').addClass('header-wrap-change');
            localStorage.setItem('setupTime', JSON.stringify({
                initial: TIMESTAMP,
                // expiresOn: TIMESTAMP + 1000 *60,
                expiresOn: TIMESTAMP + 1000*60*60*24 // 1month in ms
            }));
        });

        $('body').on('click', '.show-panduan', function (e) {
            var modal = $('body').find('#modal-apk-info');
            $(modal).modal('show');
            $('.header-wrap-apk').css("opacity", "0.7");
            $('.header-wrap').css("opacity", "0.9");
        })
        $('body').on('click', '#close-apk-info', function (e) {
            $('.header-wrap-apk').css("opacity", "1");
            $('.header-wrap').css("opacity", "1");
        })
    });

    $(document).ready(function() {
        var balance = '0.00';
        num = balance.toString().replace(/[^0-9.]/g, '');
        if (num < 1000) {
            return num;
        }
        let si = [
        {v: 1E3, s: "K"},
        // {v: 1E6, s: "M"},
        // {v: 1E9, s: "B"},
        // {v: 1E12, s: "T"},
        // {v: 1E15, s: "P"},
        // {v: 1E18, s: "E"}
        ];
        let index;
        for (index = si.length - 1; index > 0; index--) {
            if (num >= si[index].v) {
                break;
            }
        }
        // close .
        function getFlooredFixed(v, d) {
            return (Math.floor(v * Math.pow(10, d)) / Math.pow(10, d)).toFixed(d);
        }
        // add commas
        function numberWithCommas(x) {
            x = x.toString();
            var pattern = /(-?\d+)(\d{3})/;
            while (pattern.test(x))
                x = x.replace(pattern, "$1,$2");
            return x;
        }
        var to_fixed = (num / si[index].v);
        var commas = getFlooredFixed(to_fixed, 0);
        $('body').find('.m-profile .navbar-nav .profile-wrapper ul .balance-show').text('IDR: '+ numberWithCommas(commas) + ' (' + si[index].s + ')');
    })

<script>
	const slider = document.querySelector("#child");
	const preventClick = (e) => {
		e.preventDefault();
		e.stopImmediatePropagation();
	}
	let isDown = false;
	var isDragged = false;
	let startX;
	let scrollLeft;

	slider.addEventListener("mousedown", e => {
		isDown = true;
		slider.classList.add("active");
		startX = e.pageX - slider.offsetLeft;
		scrollLeft = slider.scrollLeft;
	});

	slider.addEventListener("mouseleave", () => {
		isDown = false;
		slider.classList.remove("active");
	});

	slider.addEventListener("mouseup", e => {
		isDown = false;
		const elements = document.getElementsByClassName("nav-item");
		if(isDragged){
			for(let i = 0; i<elements.length; i++){
					elements[i].addEventListener("click", preventClick);
			}
		}else{
			for(let i = 0; i<elements.length; i++){
					elements[i].removeEventListener("click", preventClick);
			}
		}
		slider.classList.remove("active");
		isDragged = false;
	});

	slider.addEventListener("mousemove", e => {
		if (!isDown) return;
		isDragged =  true;
		e.preventDefault();
		const x = e.pageX - slider.offsetLeft;
		const walk = (x - startX) * 2;
		slider.scrollLeft = scrollLeft - walk;
	});

	document.getElementsByClassName("nav-item").ondragstart = function() {};
</script>		</div>

<script>
	const togel = document.querySelector("#togel_scroll");
	const preventsClick = (e) => {
		e.preventDefault();
		e.stopImmediatePropagation();
	}
	let isDown1 = false;
	var isDragged1 = false;
	let startX1;
	let scroll;

	togel.addEventListener("mousedown", e => {
		isDown1 = true;
		togel.classList.add("active");
		startX1 = e.pageX - togel.offsetLeft;
		scroll = togel.scrollLeft;
	});

	togel.addEventListener("mouseleave", () => {
		isDown1 = false;
		togel.classList.remove("active");
	});

	togel.addEventListener("mouseup", e => {
		isDown1 = false;
		const elements = document.getElementsByClassName("nav-item-togel");
		if(isDragged1){
			for(let i = 0; i<elements.length; i++){
					elements[i].addEventListener("click", preventsClick);
			}
		}else{
			for(let i = 0; i<elements.length; i++){
					elements[i].removeEventListener("click", preventsClick);
			}
		}
		togel.classList.remove("active");
		isDragged1 = false;
	});

	togel.addEventListener("mousemove", e => {
		if (!isDown1) return;
		isDragged1 =  true;
		e.preventDefault();
		const x = e.pageX - togel.offsetLeft;
		const walk = (x - startX1) * 2;
		togel.scrollLeft = scroll - walk;
	});
</script>			</div>

	$(document).ready(function() {
		$( ".sub-arrowed" ).click( function() {
			let collaped = $( this ).find('.show').length;
			let arrow_1 = $( this ).find('.arrow-1');
			if (collaped) {
				arrow_1.animate(
					{ deg: 45 },
						{
						duration: 100,
						step: function(now) {
							$(this).css({ transform: 'rotate(' + now + 'deg)' });
						}
					}
				);
			} else {
				arrow_1.animate(
					{ deg: 135 },
						{
						duration: 100,
						step: function(now) {
							$(this).css({ transform: 'rotate(' + now + 'deg)' });
						}
					}
				);
			}
		});
	});
</script>

		<script type="text/javascript">
			setTimeout(function () {
				try {
					var livechartID = window.__lc.license;
					$('a.chart-link, a.lc-link').attr('href', 'https://lc.chat/now/'+livechartID+'/');
				}
				catch(err) {
					console.log('no live chart ID was found');
				}
			}, 200);

			// countdown maintenance time
			$(document).ready(function() {
				let _element = $('body').find('.countdown');
				let _maintenance = $('body').find('.maintain-time');

				// countdown before maintenance
				if (_element.length > 0) {
					setInterval(function() {
						let _now = moment(new Date()).tz('Asia/Bangkok');
						$.each(_element, function(value, index) {
							let _this = $(this);
							let _start = moment(_this.attr('data-countdown')).tz('Asia/Bangkok');
							let diff = moment.duration(_start.diff(_now));

							let d = pad(diff.days()) + ' d ';
							let h = pad(diff.hours()) + ' h ';
							let m = pad(diff.minutes()) + ' m ';
							let s = pad(diff.seconds()) + ' s';

							_this.find('.d').text(d);
							_this.find('.h').text(h);
							_this.find('.m').text(m);
							_this.find('.s').text(s);

							if (diff < 0) {
								_this.find('.d').text('00 d ');
								_this.find('.h').text('00 h ');
								_this.find('.m').text('00 m ');
								_this.find('.s').text('00 s');
							}
						});
					}, 1000);
				}

				// countdown during maintenance
				if (_maintenance.length > 0) {
					var count = 0;
					setInterval(function() {
						$.each(_maintenance, function(value, index) {
							let _this = $(this);
							let _starttime = new Date(_this.attr('data-start-time')).getTime();
							let _endtime = new Date(_this.attr('data-end-time')).getTime();

							var getCountdown = function(c) {
								let secondsLeft = ((_endtime - _starttime) / 1000) - c;
								days = pad(Math.floor(secondsLeft / 86400));
								secondsLeft %= 86400;
								hours = pad(Math.floor(secondsLeft / 3600));
								secondsLeft %= 3600;
								minutes = pad(Math.floor(secondsLeft / 60));
								seconds = pad(Math.floor(secondsLeft % 60));

								_this.find('.mt-day span').text(days);
								_this.find('.mt-hour span').text(hours);
								_this.find('.mt-minute span').text(minutes);
								_this.find('.mt-second span').text(seconds);

								if (secondsLeft < 0) {
									_this.find('.mt-day span').text('00');
									_this.find('.mt-hour span').text('00');
									_this.find('.mt-minute span').text('00');
									_this.find('.mt-second span').text('00');
								}
							}
							getCountdown(count);
						});
						count++;
					}, 1000);
				}

				function pad(n) {
					return (n < 10 ? '0' : '') + n;
				}
			})
		</script>
